<div class="NavHead" style="font-size: 105%; background: transparent; text-align: left; text-align:center;background-color:#efefef;">Lap leaders</div>
<ul class="NavContent" style="list-style: none none; margin-left: 0; text-align: center; font-size: 105%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; line-height: inherit;"><li style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0"><div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_1b1862297421f1644488fe957e31b489"></map><img usemap="#timeline_1b1862297421f1644488fe957e31b489" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/1b1862297421f1644488fe957e31b489.png" /></div></li></ul>
</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2013 British Grand Prix</b> (formally the <b>2013 Formula 1 Santander British Grand Prix</b>) was a <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> motor race held at the <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Circuit" title="Silverstone Circuit">Silverstone Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Silverstone" title="Silverstone">Silverstone</a>, England, United Kingdom, on 30&#160;June 2013 before 120,000 spectators. It was the eighth round of the <a href="/wiki/2013_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2013 Formula One World Championship">2013 Formula One World Championship</a> and the 64th&#160;<a href="/wiki/British_Grand_Prix" title="British Grand Prix">British Grand Prix</a> to be held as part of the series. <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> won the 52-lap race from a second position start. <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a> team finished second and <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> took third in a <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a>, Rosberg's teammate, won the <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> by setting the fastest lap in qualifying. He led for the first eight laps until his car's left-rear tyre failed on lap eight, promoting Red Bull driver <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> to the lead. Two more left-rear tyre failures for Ferrari's <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Toro_Rosso" title="Scuderia Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a> led to race director <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a> deploying the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>. The race was restarted at the end of lap&#160;21 with Vettel leading. He led for the next 20&#160;laps before a <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> failure forced him to retire on the 41st&#160;lap and cause a second safety car deployment. Rosberg took the lead, and held off Webber for the rest of the race to win. It was Rosberg's second victory of the season and the third of his career.
</p><p>A total of six tyre failures occurred during the race and supplier <a href="/wiki/Pirelli" title="Pirelli">Pirelli</a> modified them to make them less susceptible to punctures for the following <a href="/wiki/2013_German_Grand_Prix" title="2013 German Grand Prix">German Grand Prix</a> as a stop-gap solution before introducing a new tyre at the <a href="/wiki/2013_Hungarian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Hungarian Grand Prix">Hungarian Grand Prix</a>. Pirelli investigated the incidents and concluded there was no single cause. As a result of the race, Alonso moved to within 21&#160;<a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a> of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> leader Vettel. <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a> team finished fifth to remain in third and Hamilton maintained fourth place. In the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">World Constructors' Championship</a>, Mercedes overtook Ferrari, moving to within 48&#160;points behind Red Bull with eleven rounds remaining in the season.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Silverstone_Circuit,_July_2,_2018_SkySat_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="The Silverstone Circuit seen from the air" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-Silverstone_Circuit%2C_July_2%2C_2018_SkySat_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1360" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Silverstone_Circuit,_July_2,_2018_SkySat_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Circuit" title="Silverstone Circuit">Silverstone Circuit</a> <i>(pictured in 2018)</i>, where the race was held</div></div></div>
<p>The round was the eighth of the 19&#160;races in the <a href="/wiki/2013_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2013 Formula One World Championship">2013 FIA Formula One World Championship</a>, and the 64th&#160;<a href="/wiki/British_Grand_Prix" title="British Grand Prix">British Grand Prix</a> as part of the series. It was held at the 18-turn 5.891&#160;km (3.660&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Circuit" title="Silverstone Circuit">Silverstone Circuit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Silverstone" title="Silverstone">Silverstone</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northamptonshire" title="Northamptonshire">Northamptonshire</a>, England, on 30&#160;June.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Formula_One_tyres" title="Formula One tyres">Tyre</a> supplier <a href="/wiki/Pirelli" title="Pirelli">Pirelli</a> brought the white-banded medium and the orange-banded hard compound dry tyres and the green-banded <a href="/wiki/Rain_tyre" title="Rain tyre">intermediate</a> and dark blue-banded full wet tyres to the race.<sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Drag_reduction_system" title="Drag reduction system">drag reduction system</a> (DRS) was expanded from one to two activation zones for 2013:<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> one was on the Wellington <a href="/wiki/Straight_(racing)" title="Straight (racing)">Straight</a> on the entry to Brooklands corner and the second was on the Hangar Straight linking Chapel and Stowe turns. For the race, several drains to improve circuit drainage and prevent water accumulation were installed, and the outside tyre wall at the exit to Chapel Curve was extended by 50&#160;m (160&#160;ft).<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before the race, <a href="/wiki/Red_Bull_Racing" title="Red Bull Racing">Red Bull</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Drivers%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Drivers&#39; Champions">World Drivers' Championship</a> with 132&#160;<a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Championship_points_scoring_systems" title="List of Formula One World Championship points scoring systems">points</a>, ahead of <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">Ferrari</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> with 96&#160;points and <a href="/wiki/Lotus_F1" title="Lotus F1">Lotus</a>' <a href="/wiki/Kimi_R%C3%A4ikk%C3%B6nen" title="Kimi Räikkönen">Kimi Räikkönen</a> with 88&#160;points. <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz_in_Formula_One" title="Mercedes-Benz in Formula One">Mercedes</a> team was fourth with 77&#160;points and Vettel's teammate <a href="/wiki/Mark_Webber" title="Mark Webber">Mark Webber</a> was fifth with 69&#160;points.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull led the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_World_Constructors%27_Champions" title="List of Formula One World Constructors&#39; Champions">World Constructors' Championship</a> with 201&#160;points; Ferrari and Mercedes were second and third respectively, with 145&#160;and 134&#160;points. Lotus were fourth with 114&#160;points and <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a> were fifth with 51&#160;points.<sup id="cite_ref-regulations_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Vettel won the preceding <a href="/wiki/2013_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Canadian Grand Prix">Canadian Grand Prix</a> from Alonso, but did not want to speculate on the outcome at Silverstone or the championship. "Fernando was a little bit unlucky here and there and we were able to beat him, so we were able to come back but this was ten races from where we are now so I think there are so many things that can happen at that stage of the championship."<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Alonso said his team could not make more errors and lose extra points. He was confident about his prospects at Silverstone because of Ferrari's recent competitiveness there saying, "We have an interesting weekend ahead of us, but we can approach it with confidence, knowing we have a good opportunity."<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Stirling_Moss" title="Stirling Moss">Stirling Moss</a>, who won the <a href="/wiki/1955_British_Grand_Prix" title="1955 British Grand Prix">1955 British Grand Prix</a> for Mercedes, felt Hamilton could possibly win the race and Hamilton himself wanted to win at Silverstone for the second time.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton said he was looking forward to learning how his car would perform and felt Mercedes would be competitive at Silverstone.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> His teammate <a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> commented that his aim was to score points at the race.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Susie Wolff driving a F1 car exiting a turn" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg/220px-Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="122" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg/330px-Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg/440px-Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4117" data-file-height="2290" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Susie_Wolff_2013_Silverstone_F1_Test_002.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Susie_Wolff" title="Susie Wolff">Susie Wolff</a> was the first woman to drive a Formula One car in an official session since 1992 at the post-race test held at the circuit</div></div></div>
<p>The second mid-season test of 2013 was held at the circuit three weeks after the race. <a href="/wiki/Auto_GP" title="Auto GP">Auto GP</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Kimiya_Sato" title="Kimiya Sato">Kimiya Sato</a> and <a href="/wiki/GP3_Series" title="GP3 Series">GP3 Series</a> racers <a href="/wiki/Daniil_Kvyat" title="Daniil Kvyat">Daniil Kvyat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Sainz_Jr." title="Carlos Sainz Jr.">Carlos Sainz Jr.</a> made their first appearances in a Formula One test session for the <a href="/wiki/Sauber_Motorsport" title="Sauber Motorsport">Sauber</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Toro_Rosso" title="Scuderia Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> teams respectively,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> while <a href="/wiki/Renault_Sport_Series" title="Renault Sport Series">World Series by Renault</a> driver <a href="/wiki/Will_Stevens" title="Will Stevens">Will Stevens</a> drove a <a href="/wiki/Caterham_F1" title="Caterham F1">Caterham</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Marussia_F1" title="Marussia F1">Marussia</a> team entered <a href="/wiki/Tio_Ellinas" title="Tio Ellinas">Tio Ellinas</a> from the GP3&#160;Series,<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Susie_Wolff" title="Susie Wolff">Susie Wolff</a> drove a <a href="/wiki/Williams_Grand_Prix_Engineering" title="Williams Grand Prix Engineering">Williams</a> car, becoming the first woman to drive a Formula One car in an official session since <a href="/wiki/Giovanna_Amati" title="Giovanna Amati">Giovanna Amati</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="1992 Formula One World Championship">1992</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> The Mercedes team were not allowed to enter the test because the <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fédération Internationale de l&#39;Automobile">Fédération Internationale de l'Automobile</a> (FIA; Formula One's governing body) International Tribunal concluded they broke the regulations by running its 2013 car in an illegal test session with Pirelli at the <a href="/wiki/Circuit_de_Barcelona-Catalunya" title="Circuit de Barcelona-Catalunya">Circuit de Catalunya</a> a month prior.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/James_Rossiter" title="James Rossiter">James Rossiter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Force_India" title="Force India">Force India</a>'s simulator driver, was due to drive a <a href="/wiki/Force_India_VJM06" title="Force India VJM06">VJM06</a> car in lieu of <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Sutil" title="Adrian Sutil">Adrian Sutil</a> during the first free practice session to gather simulation data until inclement weather cancelled the plan.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Some teams modified their cars for the race.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Ferrari introduced a new <a href="/wiki/Spoiler_(car)" title="Spoiler (car)">rear wing</a> featured an alteration in its vertical slot in the endplate's lower front on the <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_F138" title="Ferrari F138">F138</a> car.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes installed a cable-free thermic sensor on the <a href="/wiki/Mercedes_F1_W04" title="Mercedes F1 W04">F1&#160;W04</a>'s front wing to monitor the front tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Lotus used a "double DRS" system on Räikkönen's <a href="/wiki/Lotus_E21" title="Lotus E21">E21</a>&#160;car to direct airflow and lower <a href="/wiki/Downforce" title="Downforce">downforce</a> for the first time in a race after evaluating it in Friday practice sessions in <a href="/wiki/2012_Formula_One_World_Championship" title="2012 Formula One World Championship">2012</a> and the 2013 pre-season test session.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> The team also modified the car's <a href="/wiki/Car_suspension" title="Car suspension">suspension system</a>, introduced a new front wing and multiple aerodynamic upgrades in anticipation of an improved performance.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Practice">Practice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Practice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Per the regulations for the 2013 season, three practice sessions were held, two 90-minute sessions on Friday and another 60-minute session on Saturday.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Regs_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Regs-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> The first session occurred in wet weather, which had moved in on Thursday afternoon.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Water streams formed across some turns and several drivers lost control of their cars. No one set a fast lap until after 75 minutes since teams were reluctant to send drivers onto the wet track.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Ricciardo" title="Daniel Ricciardo">Daniel Ricciardo</a> of the Toro Rosso team set the fastest lap, a 1-minute, 54.249 seconds, ahead of Sauber's <a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a>, Williams driver <a href="/wiki/Pastor_Maldonado" title="Pastor Maldonado">Pastor Maldonado</a>, Hamilton, Sauber's <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Guti%C3%A9rrez" title="Esteban Gutiérrez">Esteban Gutiérrez</a> and Maldonado's teammate <a href="/wiki/Valtteri_Bottas" title="Valtteri Bottas">Valtteri Bottas</a> in positions two to six. <a href="/wiki/Charles_Pic" title="Charles Pic">Charles Pic</a> lost control of the rear of his Caterham and collided with the barrier at Club turn, removing the front wing. Gutiérrez <a href="/wiki/Aquaplaning" title="Aquaplaning">aquaplaned</a> at the first corner but regained control of his car.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Conditions improved as the rain showers eased up. The <a href="/wiki/GP2_Series" title="GP2 Series">GP2 Series</a> practice session removed some standing water, allowing drivers to head out as the second session began. Drivers used intermediate tyres early on, but used dry tyres after ten minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP2_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP2-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg recorded the day's fastest lap, a 1-minute, 32.248 seconds, with 40 minutes left in the session.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP2_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP2-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> The Red Bull duo of Webber and Vettel, Force India's <a href="/wiki/Paul_di_Resta" title="Paul di Resta">Paul di Resta</a>, Hamilton, Ricciardo and his Toro Rosso teammate <a href="/wiki/Jean-%C3%89ric_Vergne" title="Jean-Éric Vergne">Jean-Éric Vergne</a>, Sutil, Lotus' <a href="/wiki/Romain_Grosjean" title="Romain Grosjean">Romain Grosjean</a> and Alonso followed in positions two to ten.<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP2_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP2-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP2_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP2-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> was limited to seven timed laps because he lost control of the rear of his Ferrari on a damp area at the exit of Stowe corner,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportFP2_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportFP2-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP2_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP2-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FP2_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FP2-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> damaging the front suspension sliding across the inside tyre barrier before stopping at the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a> entry.<sup id="cite_ref-F1FP2_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FP2-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the session, Hamilton was summoned to the stewards and received his first reprimand of the season for not complying with their instructions to remain to the right of a <a href="/wiki/Bollard" title="Bollard">bollard</a> for safety reasons entering the pit lane.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> In the final session, which took place in clear and warmer weather and saw both dry compound tyres used,<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP3_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP3-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg was again fastest with a 1-minute, 31.487 seconds lap. Hamilton, Vettel, Webber, Grosjean, Ricciardo, Alonso, Räikkönen, Sutil and Di Resta completed the top ten.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP3_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP3-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> McLaren's <a href="/wiki/Sergio_P%C3%A9rez" title="Sergio Pérez">Sergio Pérez</a> sustained a left-front <a href="/wiki/Flat_tire" title="Flat tire">tyre puncture</a> at the exit to Copse turn,<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNFP3_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNFP3-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> which was caused by an unidentified object creating a large cut in the wheel's sidewall and damaging the car's floor. Officials <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Red_flag" title="Racing flags">stopped</a> the session briefly after 13 minutes to clean the track.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Pérez's car was repaired for him to drive the final ten minutes before he spun backwards at Becketts Curve.<sup id="cite_ref-GPFP3_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GPFP3-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying">Qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Lewis Hamilton wearing sunglasses looking off to his left" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg/170px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="243" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg/255px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg/340px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg 2x" data-file-width="895" data-file-height="1280" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton" title="Lewis Hamilton">Lewis Hamilton</a> took the 28th <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> of his career in qualifying.</div></div></div>
<p>Saturday afternoon's <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#Q" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">qualifying session</a> was divided into three parts. The first 18-minute session eliminated cars that finished 17th or lower. The <a href="/wiki/107%25_rule" title="107% rule">107%&#160;rule</a> was in effect, requiring drivers to reach a time within 107 per cent of the quickest lap to qualify. The second 15-minute session eliminated cars that finished 11th to 16th. The final ten-minute session determined <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">pole position</a> to tenth. Cars that progressed to the final session were not allowed to change tyres for the race's start, using the tyres with which they set their quickest lap times in the third session.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Regs_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Regs-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton took his second pole position of the season and the 28th of his career with a time of 1 minute, 29.607 seconds on his final lap.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashQuali_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashQuali-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He was joined on the <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a>'s front row by his teammate Rosberg, who battled his teammate for pole position.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Mercedes took its first front row lockout at Silverstone since <a href="/wiki/Juan_Manuel_Fangio" title="Juan Manuel Fangio">Juan Manuel Fangio</a> and Moss in 1955 and its third of 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Vettel took third and Webber was fourth after an error braking for Club corner lost him time.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CrashQuali_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashQuali-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Di Resta and Sutil for Force India took fifth and seventh on a new set of medium tyres; Ricciardo separated the duo in sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Grosjean in eighth had an <a href="/wiki/Understeer_and_oversteer" title="Understeer and oversteer">understeer</a> on his final timed lap at turn 15,<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> and his teammate Räikkönen in ninth had issues on the medium tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alonso, tenth, switched from the hard to the medium compound tyres with the intention of entering the pit lane if his lap was poor.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Button took 11th after he failed to progress to the final session by one-tenth of a second because he required a hard <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#O" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">out-lap</a> to generate tyre temperature.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> 12th-placed Massa was unable to set a fast enough lap after the loss of track time changing his engine after his crash the day before.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_42-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Vergne, 13th, ran wide at the exit of Becketts Curve on his fastest lap, possibly because of the aerodynamic turbulence of airflow over Vettel's car removing downforce and causing him to make an error. Pérez, 14th, had irrecoverable tyre temperature from being randomly instructed to drive onto the FIA weighbridge and traffic slowing him.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_42-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Hülkenberg took 15th on his final lap ahead of the Williams duo of Maldonado and Bottas.<sup id="cite_ref-CrashQuali_40-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CrashQuali-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Gutiérrez in 18th lost time exiting the corners. An improved car balance put Pic 19th, and Marussia's <a href="/wiki/Jules_Bianchi" title="Jules Bianchi">Jules Bianchi</a> drove his improved car to 20th. Van Der Garde and Marussia's <a href="/wiki/Max_Chilton" title="Max Chilton">Max Chilton</a> were 21st and 22nd respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-QualiQuotes_42-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-QualiQuotes-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-qualifying">Post-qualifying</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Post-qualifying">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After the session, the FIA technical delegate <a href="/wiki/Jo_Bauer" title="Jo Bauer">Jo Bauer</a> found Di Resta and his Force India car without fuel to be 1.5&#160;kg (3.3&#160;lb) under the minimum weight limit of 642&#160;kg (1,415&#160;lb) and reported him to the stewards. They decided Force India broke series' regulations and ordered Di Resta to start from 22nd. The Force India team did not appeal the decision.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNDIRPenalty_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNDIRPenalty-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCDIRPenalty_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDIRPenalty-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Van Der Garde was demoted five grid positions after the stewards concluded that he had collided with Hülkenberg at the preceding Canadian Grand Prix.<sup id="cite_ref-VDGFirstPenalty_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VDGFirstPenalty-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> A second five-place grid penalty was imposed on him because Caterham broke a seal to change his <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> <a href="/wiki/Layshaft" title="Layshaft">layshaft</a> after qualifying.<sup id="cite_ref-NBCSecondVDGPenalty_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBCSecondVDGPenalty-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Qualifying_classification">Qualifying classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Qualifying classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The fastest lap in each of the three sessions is denoted in <b>bold</b>.

<p><b>Notes:</b>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_1"><b><a href="#ref_1">^1</a></b></span> &#160;— <a href="/wiki/Paul_di_Resta" title="Paul di Resta">Paul di Resta</a> was excluded from qualifying and sent to the back of the <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_motorsport_terms#G" title="Glossary of motorsport terms">grid</a> because he and his car were found to be under the minimum weight limit of 640&#160;kg (1,410&#160;lb).<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNDIRPenalty_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNDIRPenalty-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBCDIRPenalty_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDIRPenalty-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_2"><b><a href="#ref_2">^2</a></b></span> &#160;— <a href="/wiki/Giedo_van_der_Garde" title="Giedo van der Garde">Giedo van der Garde</a> was imposed a five-place grid penalty for causing an accident with <a href="/wiki/Nico_H%C3%BClkenberg" title="Nico Hülkenberg">Nico Hülkenberg</a> at the preceding <a href="/wiki/2013_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Canadian Grand Prix">Canadian Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-VDGFirstPenalty_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VDGFirstPenalty-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> He later incurred a second five-place grid penalty because the Caterham team had changed his <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-NBCSecondVDGPenalty_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NBCSecondVDGPenalty-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Race">Race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The 52-lap race took place in the afternoon of 30 June from 14:00 local time.<sup id="cite_ref-FIAPreview_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIAPreview-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> The weather at the start was clear with the air temperature between 21 to 22&#160;°C (70 to 72&#160;°F) and a track temperature from 29 to 34&#160;°C (84 to 93&#160;°F);<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> a gusty wind was present,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and no rain was forecast.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> 120,000 attended the event.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> The first nine starters began on the medium compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> The optimum strategy was for a driver to make three pit stops because it was faster and not be impeded by slower traffic.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton made a brisk start to lead the field into the first corner. Vettel overtook the slow-starting Rosberg for second.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Webber and Grosjean made contact through Abbey corner, damaging the former's <a href="/wiki/Carbon_fiber_reinforced_polymer" title="Carbon fiber reinforced polymer">carbon fibre</a> front wing, and driving onto the <a href="/wiki/Run-off_area" title="Run-off area">run-off area</a> and fell to 14th&#160;position.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Sutil progressed from sixth to fourth place,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and Massa moved through traffic to go from eleventh to fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Driving towards Stowe turn, Alonso overtook Button on the inside for ninth. Hamilton led Vettel by eight-tenths of a second by the end of the first lap, with Rosberg third and Sutil fourth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton began to pull away from Vettel,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> his car was faster all round the track.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Alonso discovered his Ferrari was better in cooler weather because of a favourable car balance. He passed Grosjean for eighth at the exit of Woodcote corner at the start on lap two after Grosjean ran wide at turn three, the result of his contact with Webber.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton was two seconds ahead of Vettel by lap five, preventing Vettel from using DRS and allowing Hamilton to react a pit stop without losing position.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> That same lap, Alonso switched lines in an unsuccessful attempt to pass Ricciardo into Stowe corner and Grosjean caught up to him. By lap seven, Webber had recovered from 14th to 11th.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Lewis Hamilton driving into the pit lane" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/220px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/330px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/440px-Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6000" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lewis_Hamilton_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Lewis Hamilton driving into the <a href="/wiki/Pit_stop" title="Pit stop">pit lane</a> on lap eight after sustaining a left-rear tyre failure while in first position</div></div></div>
<p>After exiting turn five on lap eight,<sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton's rear left tyre punctured and rapidly deflated on the Wellington Straight.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Tyre rubber flew off the wheel and littered the track as Vettel swerved to avoid hitting it and took over the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton drove slowly to the pit lane for a replacement wheel and checks to his car; the wheel's sidewall stayed intact and fibres flailed on it.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> He rejoined the race on the hard compound tyres in 22nd; <a href="/wiki/Racing_flags#Yellow_flags" title="Racing flags">yellow flags</a> were waved to warn drivers about on-track debris.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> One lap later, Alonso exited Stowe corner with a punctured right-rear tyre that did not delaminate, causing him to enter the pit lane for the hard compound tyres, falling to 11th. His teammate Massa, in fourth, sustained the race's third tyre failure on lap ten when his left rear wheel deflated in Aintree corner, spinning onto the run-off area.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Massa entered the pit lane cautiously for a new set of tyres and fell to 22nd.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Because of debris on the Wellington Straight, DRS was disabled on lap 11,<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> and it was around this point that FIA race director <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Whiting" title="Charlie Whiting">Charlie Whiting</a> considered stopping the race but decided not to.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pirelli technicians took the rear tyre rubber to their garage for analysis, advised teams to raise pressures to 24&#160;psi (170&#160;kPa) and told drivers to avoid mounting the kerbs.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Between laps&#160;12 and&#160;13, Alonso overtook the Lotus duo of Räikkönen and Grosjean on the Hangar Straight and Vergne into Brooklands corner to move into sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Grosjean blocked his teammate Räikkönen from passing him at Maggots corner.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull called Vettel into the pit lane for his first pit stop on the 13th&#160;lap and retained the lead. On lap&#160;14, the Lotus team asked Grosjean to allow his teammate Räikkönen into sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> As he did so on the Hangar Straight linking Stowe corner,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Vergne's left-rear tyre failed at 180&#160;mph (290&#160;km/h) and littered debris on the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> A large piece of tyre landed on Räikkönen's helmet, without causing him injury. Vergne entered the pit lane to switch to a new set of hard compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> This fourth tyre failure along with tyre debris on the circuit caused Whiting to deploy the <a href="/wiki/Safety_car" title="Safety car">safety car</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Felipe Massa driving to the pit lane" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/220px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/330px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg/440px-Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6000" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Felipe_Massa_2013_Britain_Race.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">Felipe Massa</a> on his way to the pit lane to replace a failed left-rear tyre</div></div></div>
<p>As <a href="/wiki/Motorsport_marshal" title="Motorsport marshal">track marshals</a> checked and cleared on-track debris with road clearing trucks,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Vettel was told by radio the inside of his left-rear medium compound tyre that he began the race on had sustained cuts to it.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Teams sought to lessen the amount of time spent on their tyres when the switch to making three stops became common.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> The safety car was withdrawn at the end of the 21st&#160;lap,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and racing resumed with Vettel leading Rosberg and Sutil.<sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Pérez overtook Webber on the inside into Abbey corner for eighth.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Webber, whose front wing was changed earlier,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> retook eighth from Pérez on the inside at Brooklands turn. On lap 28, Ricciardo turned left into the same turn and passed Grosjean for sixth place.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Gutiérrez front-left tyre's was punctured from a cut on the Hangar Straight linking Stowe corner on lap&#160;28.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> The tyre, which did not delaminate,<sup id="cite_ref-TyreFailures_54-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TyreFailures-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> damaged his front wing,<sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> and left carbon fibre debris on the track.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Alonso, who was close by Sutil, swerved to avoid the debris.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On that lap, Webber overtook Grosjean into Brooklands corner for seventh.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>The second round of pit stops commenced on the 30th&#160;lap. Räikkönen, Grosjean and Alonso were the first of the leaders to enter the pit lane for the hard compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> As he was released, Alonso was forced to brake to avoid hitting Grosjean's car as he entered his pit stall, allowing Räikkönen past him.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Over laps&#160;31 and 32, Hamilton attempted two unsuccessful passes on Di Resta on the main straight and into Brooklands corner.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Sutil and Rosberg made their second pit stops for the hard compound tyres over laps&#160;33 and&#160;34.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> On lap&#160;35, Webber used DRS on the Hangar Straight into Stowe corner to pass Alonso for fourth position.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Vettel made his second pit stop from the lead on the same lap for hard compound tyres.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> He retained the lead.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On the 36th&#160;lap, Di Resta and Hülkenberg made contact in turn tree, damaging the former's front wing. After Hamilton exited the pit lane on the next lap, Di Resta passed him.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Hamilton attempted to pass Di Resta again before Stowe corner. Instead, he narrowly avoided a rearward collision with the rear of Di Resta's car on lap&#160;37.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> That same lap,<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Toro Rosso retired Vergne in the pit lane with significant damage to his car.<sup id="cite_ref-RaceQuotes_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RaceQuotes-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sebastian Vettel walking away from his stricken car parked next to the pit wall" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg/220px-Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg/330px-Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg/440px-Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4800" data-file-height="3200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sebastian_Vettel_and_his_RB9_2013_Britain.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> retired from the lead of the race on the 41st lap with a <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(mechanics)" title="Transmission (mechanics)">gearbox</a> failure.</div></div></div>
<p>Hamilton overtook Di Resta for 11th at the exit of turn three on the following lap. Button passed Grosjean into Brooklands corner for ninth on lap&#160;39. Ricciardo attempted to pass Sutil into Copse corner for sixth but Sutil blocked him by switching lines, slowing Ricciardo. On lap 41, Hamilton used DRS to pass Grosjean on the Hangar Straight for tenth <sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On that lap, Vettel went to change to fifth gear into Vale corner when he lost drive. He drove slowly round Club turn and stopped at the side of the main straight next to pit wall to retire for the first time in 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> This promoted Rosberg to the lead, Räikkönen to second and Webber to third.<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> With Vettel's car deemed to be in a dangerous position, the safety car was deployed for the second time to allow his car to be moved safely from the track.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-F1FanaticRace_55-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1FanaticRace-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>The safety car created a situation in which teams had to decide whether to make a pit stop to keep or gain position with nine laps to go. Rosberg and Webber made their stops at the end of&#160;lap 42 for the hard and medium tyres, respectively. Rosberg retained the lead as Webber fell to fifth. Räikkönen, Sutil and Ricciardo in positions two to four remained on the circuit.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg was informed by radio of an issue with the centre of his left-rear tyre. Racing resumed at the conclusion of lap&#160;45 when the safety car entered the pit lane.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Webber overtook Ricciardo into Brooklands turn for fourth on lap&#160;46, and Alonso passed Button for seventh into Copse turn.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Entering the Hangar Straight, Alonso was <a href="/wiki/Drafting_(aerodynamics)" title="Drafting (aerodynamics)">slipstreaming</a> Pérez at 179&#160;mph (288&#160;km/h) when Perez's left-rear tyre failed without warning and damaged his floor. Alonso turned right to avoid tyre debris from Pérez's car littering the track, as McLaren retired the latter in the pit lane.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-RaceQuotes_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RaceQuotes-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Mico Rosberg driving into a turn" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg/220px-Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg/330px-Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg/440px-Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4800" data-file-height="3200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Nico_Rosberg_2013_Britain_FP3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Nico_Rosberg" title="Nico Rosberg">Nico Rosberg</a> took the third victory of his career</div></div></div>
<p>On lap&#160;47, Hamilton overtook Button for seventh and Webber deployed DRS to pass Sutil for third. Webber passed Räikkönen with DRS for second at Copse corner on the following lap, just as Ricciardo lost fourth to Alonso.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On the 49th&#160;lap,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Alonso and Hamilton demoted Sutil to fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Alonso had DRS available on lap&#160;50 and used the extra grip in his tyres to pass Räikkönen for third. On the next lap, Hamilton used DRS to pass Räikkönen for fourth place.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On the final lap, the Lotus team retired Grosjean in the pit lane because of front wing damage slowing him,<sup id="cite_ref-AutosportReview_2-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AutosportReview-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-RaceQuotes_56-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RaceQuotes-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> just as Massa overtook Sutil for sixth.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPNRaceLive_50-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPNRaceLive-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg held off Webber to take his second victory of the season and the third of his career, by seven-tenths of a second.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Alonso took third, with Hamilton, Räikkönen, Massa, Sutil and Ricciardo in fourth to eighth.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcwebrace_51-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcwebrace-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-telegraphrace_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-telegraphrace-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Di Resta was ninth after a late-race error,<sup id="cite_ref-autosportrace_52-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autosportrace-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> and Hülkenberg tenth after a slow puncture required him to make a pit stop earlier than scheduled.<sup id="cite_ref-RaceQuotes_56-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RaceQuotes-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> The final finishers were Maldonado, Bottas, Button, Gutiérrez, Pic, Bianchi, Chilton and Van Der Garde.<sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-race">Post-race</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Post-race">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Damon Hill on a stage interviewing three drivers" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg/220px-Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg/330px-Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg/440px-Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4896" data-file-height="3672" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Podium_2013_British_GP.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The post-race podium ceremony with the drivers interviewed by 1996 world champion <a href="/wiki/Damon_Hill" title="Damon Hill">Damon Hill</a></div></div></div>
<p>At the podium interviews, conducted by 1996 world champion <a href="/wiki/Damon_Hill" title="Damon Hill">Damon Hill</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Rosberg called it "a very, very special day" because of the progress the Mercedes team had made over the season.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Webber said his team would have to investigate his slow start to the race and would have preferred more laps to have a chance of winning it.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Alonso said he felt it was a lucky race for his team due to the loss of position after making a pit stop during the second safety car period..<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_59-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> In the post-race press conference, Rosberg said he would not been able to catch and pass Vettel had the latter not retired due to a lack of overall speed. Webber said he was happy with his own performance and was looking forward to the next round.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_59-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Alonso called the finish "a fantastic result for our very difficult weekend" because his car was inconsistent during a meeting—slow in qualifying but fast in a race.<sup id="cite_ref-PressConf_59-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PressConf-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Rosberg was summoned to the stewards to explain a perceived non-compliance of rules for not slowing enough for waved yellow flags and not overtaking early in the race between turns three and five.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> They reviewed telemetry and broadcast footage and imposed a reprimand on Rosberg.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Vettel was disappointed to lose a potential victory with his gearbox failing late in the race, saying: "These things unfortunately happen but fortunately we've got the next race coming up next week so we can try again."<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Räikkönen said his team Lotus had made a strategy error dropping him from second to fifth in the final laps: "It's three races now where we haven't had the result we maybe expect, but hopefully if we can have a bit more luck and also get rid of some of the mistakes we'll be able to get back to the front."<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> The team's head of trackside operations Alan Permane confirmed they had made an strategy error.<sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Di Resta believed his team Force India would be happy to finish ninth and Ricciardo saw his eighth-place finish as "a missed opportunity to score more points" due to the fast pace of his car.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Button on used, cold tyres said he was "a sitting duck" because he was vulnerable to being overtaken after the safety car was deployed: "I was just waiting for people to pass me. It was tough."<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> The race result kept Vettel atop the World Drivers' Championship with 132 points. Alonso's third-place finish allowed him to close up to 21 points. Räikkönen maintained third position, Hamilton fourth, and Webber fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Red Bull maintained their lead in the World Constructors' Championship with 219 points. The points Mercedes had accrued at Silverstone allowed them to overtake Ferrari for second position. Lotus maintained fourth place and Force India were in fifth with eleven races of the season remaining.<sup id="cite_ref-2013Points_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013Points-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tyre_concerns">Tyre concerns</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Tyre concerns">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The number of tyre failures during the race overshadowed Rosberg's victory. The press likened the situation to the <a href="/wiki/2005_United_States_Grand_Prix" title="2005 United States Grand Prix">2005 United States Grand Prix</a>, when seven teams running <a href="/wiki/Michelin" title="Michelin">Michelin</a> tyres were required to withdraw over safety concerns because their tyres were deemed unusable for racing, leaving six <a href="/wiki/Bridgestone" title="Bridgestone">Bridgestone</a>-shod cars to compete.<sup id="cite_ref-F1MagAug13_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-F1MagAug13-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> A total of 20&#160;tyre failures during the season caused the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Prix_Drivers%27_Association" title="Grand Prix Drivers&#39; Association">Grand Prix Drivers' Association</a> to write a letter to <a href="/wiki/Jean_Todt" title="Jean Todt">Jean Todt</a>, the FIA president, demanding action. Button, Vettel and Ferrari test driver <a href="/wiki/Pedro_de_la_Rosa" title="Pedro de la Rosa">Pedro de la Rosa</a> met Todt to express their concerns to him.<sup id="cite_ref-DTPostRace_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTPostRace-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After several drivers and senior Formula One personnel asked for further action to be taken and had raised their concerns to the media,<sup id="cite_ref-DTPostRace_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DTPostRace-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Todt ordered tyre supplier Pirelli to be present at a meeting of the Sporting Working Committee with team principals at the <a href="/wiki/N%C3%BCrburgring" title="Nürburgring">Nürburgring</a> on 3&#160;July to propose new measures to prevent similar incidents from reoccurring in the long-term.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He had already asked Pirelli Motorsport director <a href="/wiki/Paul_Hembery" title="Paul Hembery">Paul Hembery</a>, racing manager Mario Isola and Whiting to attend a meeting in the Silverstone paddock on the night after the race.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Pirelli agreed to increase the strength of its tyres by changing the internal belts material from steel to flexible reinforced <a href="/wiki/Kevlar" title="Kevlar">kevlar</a> fibre to lessen the possibility of a puncture as a stop-gap solution for the following <a href="/wiki/2013_German_Grand_Prix" title="2013 German Grand Prix">German Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> The company received permission to introduce a new tyre featuring a combination of compound from 2012 and one from 2013 in time for the <a href="/wiki/2013_Hungarian_Grand_Prix" title="2013 Hungarian Grand Prix">Hungarian Grand Prix</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-REPunctures_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-REPunctures-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> The FIA restricted the practice of changing the left- and right-hand tyres around and limited <a href="/wiki/Camber_angle" title="Camber angle">camber</a> and tyre pressures.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At its headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">Milan</a>, Pirelli conducted its own investigation into the tyre failures observed during the race.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> The company concluded the failures were caused by incorrectly mounted rear tyres to attempt to regulate wear, low enough pressures subjecting tyres to additional stress, extreme camber angles on the suspension of cars and aggressive high kerbs. Pirelli emphasised the practice of incorrectly mounted tyres was not forbidden by the company but underestimated by all. It asked an FIA delegate to ensure teams did not under-inflate tyres and add excess camber angles on all cars.<sup id="cite_ref-REPunctures_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-REPunctures-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Race_classification">Race classification</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2013_British_Grand_Prix&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Race classification">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
